<p>"<b>Death in Bloom</b>" is the seventeenth episode in the second season of <i><a href="/wiki/Adventure_Time" title="Adventure Time">Adventure Time</a></i>. It is the forty-third episode overall.
</p>
<nav id="toc" class="toc"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Synopsis">Synopsis</span></h2>
<p>After killing <a href="/wiki/Princess_Bubblegum" title="Princess Bubblegum">Princess Bubblegum</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Princess_Plant" title="Princess Plant">Princess Plant</a> when left to take care of it, <a href="/wiki/Finn" title="Finn">Finn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jake" title="Jake">Jake</a> have to go to the <a href="/wiki/Land_of_the_Dead" title="Land of the Dead">Land of the Dead</a> in order to get its soul back.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Plot">Plot</span></h2>
<p>The episode begins with <a href="/wiki/Princess_Bubblegum" title="Princess Bubblegum">Princess Bubblegum</a> asking if <a href="/wiki/Finn" title="Finn">Finn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jake" title="Jake">Jake</a> will take care of her <a href="/wiki/Princess_Plant" title="Princess Plant">Princess Plant</a> while she is away at the <a href="/wiki/Science_Conference" title="Science Conference">Science Conference</a> in <a href="/wiki/Veggie_Village" title="Veggie Village">Veggie Village</a>. She tells them she will be back "on the Morrow," then screeches to summon a giant eagle-like bird to carry her to the conference. Finn and Jake take horrible care of the plant, shoving cookies and pizza into its soil and flowers, not watering it, and accidentally setting it on fire while reading it a story beside a fireplace. As they say goodnight to the plant, they realize it is dead and Finn suggests they go to the land of the dead and reclaim its soul before Princess Bubblegum returns from the convention. <a href="/wiki/Peppermint_Butler" title="Peppermint Butler">Peppermint Butler</a> overhears this and offers to open a portal to the Underworld for a small price "which they can discuss later" which they agree to.
</p><p>As Finn and Jake go through the portal, Peppermint Butler tells them to say "hi" to <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">Death</a> for him, trying to warn them not to drink the water, but is unable to finish before the portal closes. After viewing the terrifying environment of The Land of the Dead, Jake offers to carry Finn in his paunch while he stretches them down to the ground, but they spot an escalator instead, and they both escalate down to the entrance. Finn and Jake then run into a gatekeeper who admits people to the land of the dead. Not believing their cause of death ("because we're awesome"), the gatekeeper tells them to step out of line, but Finn and Jake walk past him, which the gatekeeper is unable to stop. Next, Finn and Jake come across skeletons that try to kill them for their flesh. Finn and Jake try to fight them off in vain, when Jake enlarges and says "I'm not a banana!" the skeletons are shaken off for a while. They are able to put themselves back together when knocked apart. Finn and Jake run away and hide in a hole from the skeletons, troubled at their slow progress at getting the Princess Plant's soul back, but Finn is somewhat relieved by the fact that Princess Bubblegum will not return until tomorrow. Jake reveals that Princess Bubblegum's statement is that she will be back "on the Morrow" and does not mean she will be back tomorrow, but that she will be riding her eagle which is named "The Morrow," which he claims is extremely fast, and would only take them about 20 minutes to return home from the Science Conference.
</p><p>Finn rushes out of the hole, sneaking past the skeletons that are still looking for them, and stops on a bridge crossing over some searching skeletons. Finn says to Jake to be very quiet, but suddenly, Jake farts with an extremely loud echo, alerting the skeletons to their position but also triggering an avalanche which double-kills them all. The last obstacle separating Finn and Jake from Death's castle is a river, which a <a href="/wiki/Talking_Skull" title="Talking Skull">talking skull</a> urges Jake to drink from after he tells Finn how thirsty he is. Sensing the skull is up to something, Finn warns Jake not to drink the water, which makes the skull say "<i>don't</i> drink the water." Reasoning that by Finn's logic this means the water is good, Jake drinks from the river and immediately forgets who he is. Not knowing who Finn is, Jake becomes uncooperative, but since they're running out of time, Finn drags him forcibly to Death's castle. As they enter the castle, Death is tending his zen garden and notices Jake hiding behind a tree and shouts "Hey. Hey! I see you!" Jake ask for Death's name, and Death asks for Jake's name, but Jake does not know his name and asks for Death's name again, forcing Death to tell him to leave, but Jake replies that he did not know he was trespassing, leaving Death distracted as Finn jumps out and announces they are not leaving until he gives back the plant's soul and Jake's memory. Death becomes more irritated as he cannot stand Finn and Jake on his property, telling them to leave. Finn then tries to kick Death, but to no avail.
</p><p>Death challenges Finn to a musical battle for the soul and memories, with Death picking a drum set with double bass pedals as his instrument while Finn picks sleigh bells. Death's performance is a heavy metal show complete with pyrotechnics while Finn's is simply shaking and stomping on the sleigh bells, so when they go to Jake to judge the winner he chooses "skeleton guy by a landslide." Death traps Finn in a magical barrier and informs him that the penalty for losing a musical battle is losing your life.
</p><p>About to die, Finn tells Death that Peppermint Butler said hi, which makes Death release Finn and remark "What?! You know Peppermint Butler?!" and lets them have whatever they want. He restores Jake's memory with the Kiss of Death and sends the flower's soul back to its body, then transports Finn and Jake back to <a href="/wiki/Land_of_Ooo" title="Land of Ooo">Ooo</a> just in time to meet Princess Bubblegum. She eats a flower from the plant, her hairstyle magically changes, and she thanks Finn and Jake with a group hug. Peppermint Butler takes this opportunity to inform them that the payment for his services will be their flesh, to which the duo think he is only kidding, to which he tells them, as his eyes start to glow eerily, he will take it from them as they sleep. Finn and Jake's smiles slowly turn to frowns, and the episode ends.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>Princess Bubblegum's <a href="/wiki/Science_Conference" title="Science Conference">Science Conference</a> takes place at Stanley's house, which is referred to as being in <a href="/wiki/Veggie_Village" title="Veggie Village">Veggie Village</a>.
</li><li>There are 20 different police cars littering the underworld.
</li><li>When the Gate Guardian tells the "spear in the neck" skeleton that he may enter, the skeleton does a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Handspring_(gymnastics)" class="extiw exitstitial" title="wikipedia:Handspring (gymnastics)">front handspring</a> through the gate.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Episode_connections">Episode connections</span></h3>
<ul><li>Finn says that he is not the musical type, but in "<a href="/wiki/Prisoners_of_Love" title="Prisoners of Love">Prisoners of Love</a>," he is seen playing the flute. In this episode, Finn chooses the sleigh bells instead.
</li><li>When Finn tells Death that he knows Peppermint Butler, the same music from the episode "<a href="/wiki/Dungeon_(episode)" title="Dungeon (episode)">Dungeon</a>" plays in the background.
</li><li>The secret room scene was re-used from "<a href="/wiki/The_Enchiridion!_(episode)" title="The Enchiridion! (episode)">The Enchiridion!</a>"
</li><li>Stanley the watermelon was first seen in "<a href="/wiki/The_Jiggler" title="The Jiggler">The Jiggler</a>.
</li><li>In the end of this episode <a href="/wiki/Peppermint_Butler" title="Peppermint Butler">Peppermint Butler</a> tells Finn and Jake that he wants their flesh as payment for helping them. This is the second time one of the candy people craves flesh, with the first being <a href="/wiki/Starchie" title="Starchie" class="mw-redirect">Starchie</a> in the episode "<a href="/wiki/Slumber_Party_Panic" title="Slumber Party Panic">Slumber Party Panic</a>," where he says that he cannot help it and continues to chew on Finn's leg.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cultural_references">Cultural references</span></h3>
<ul><li>When Peppermint Butler opens the portal into the underworld, this may be reference to Frank Belknap Long's story <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Hounds_of_Tindalos" class="extiw exitstitial" title="wikipedia:The Hounds of Tindalos">The Hounds of Tindalos</a></i> in which otherworldly evil beasts can manifest or be summoned via 90Â° angles and corners of rooms.
</li><li>When Jake drinks water from the river, he forgets who he is. This is a reference to the river <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lethe" class="extiw exitstitial" title="wikipedia:Lethe">Lethe</a> in Greek mythology.
</li></ul>
<div class="floatright"><a href="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110904031422/adventuretimewithfinnandjake/images/f/f1/KissofDeath.JPG" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="KissofDeath"  	class="lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="KissofDeath.JPG" 	data-image-name="KissofDeath.JPG" 	 data-src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110904031422/adventuretimewithfinnandjake/images/thumb/f/f1/KissofDeath.JPG/100px-KissofDeath.JPG"  	 width="100"  	 height="83"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="http://img3.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20110904031422/adventuretimewithfinnandjake/images/thumb/f/f1/KissofDeath.JPG/100px-KissofDeath.JPG" 	 alt="KissofDeath"  	class="" 	 	data-image-key="KissofDeath.JPG" 	data-image-name="KissofDeath.JPG" 	 	 width="100"  	 height="83"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a></div>
<ul><li>While Jake receives the Kiss of Death, his leg is bent behind him in a way that was used by women in old cinema and TV kissing scenes. This act is meant to signify the woman's enjoyment of the kiss.
</li><li>When Finn reveals himself to Death, Death grumbles "Another one." This may be a reference to Orpheus, who similarly came to the Underworld to reclaim a dead soul.
</li><li>To get the soul and Jake's memories back, Death challenges Finn to a musical duel. This is probably a reference to the song "The Devil Went Down to Georgia."
</li><li> Death maintains a Japanese Rock Garden, often called a Zen Garden. Zen Gardens are intended to imitate the intimate essence of nature, and to serve as an aid to meditation about the true meaning of life.
</li><li> Death gives Jake the "Kiss of Death", which is a sign given by aÂ mafiosoÂ bossÂ orÂ capoÂ that signifies that a member of the crime family has been marked for death, usually as a result of some perceived betrayal.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Errors">Errors</span></h3>
<ul><li>When Peppermint Butler is crossing his eyes, his bow tie is blue instead of red.
</li><li>When Jake asks Finn to hop in his pouch, one of Jake's arms is partially transparent.
</li><li>In the scene where Peppermint Butler opens the portal to the Land of the Dead, there is a lamp in the corner before he enters the room. It is missing when he walks to open the portal.
</li><li>While opening the portal to the Land of the Dead, Peppermint Butler is holding Finn and Jake's hands, but in the next shot he is standing behind them.
</li><li>When Finn says "No! I still have to rescue stuff," his mouth is not synced.
</li><li>When Finn and Jake lie near the slide-like path, Jake's tail cannot be seen for most of the time.
</li><li> While the Princess Plant is lying on the bed, it is about the size of the bed. However, when Jake covers it with the pillow, it is less than half the size of the bed.
</li><li> When Finn says "It's bone-kickin' time!", his right butt cheek is on his thigh.
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Production_notes">Production notes</span></h3>
<ul><li>This episode was previously titled "Dead Flower."
</li></ul>
